posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:I stayed at Wanda Realm in Wuhan on a business trip when it just opened. At that time, I didn't have any special feelings because of the rush of the schedule. This time, I took my family back to Wuhan to visit my grandmother because she was sick. My mother had to go to the hospital to take care of my grandmother. For convenience, I chose a hotel close to my parents to live, which gave me an experience beyond my expectations.

The lobby of Wanda Realm in Shanghai uses Klimt-style Bund tile paintings - the magnificent and luxurious, while Wuhan uses the scenery of East Lake, which has a more vast and majestic feeling of swallowing Yunmeng. The executive lake view room opens the curtains to a corner of East Lake, and the aesthetics are indeed thoughtful.

The decoration of the room is old-fashioned and elegant, and the electric massage chair does not increase the cost too much, but it is an extra bonus. The children like this room so much that they don't want to go anywhere on the last day and have to stay in the hotel. In addition, it should be praised that the hotel swimming pool has swimming caps and goggles that can be borrowed, which provides great convenience for guests who want to swim on a whim.

Although the dishes in the executive restaurant are not many like all hotels, the ingredients are fresh and the finished products are exquisite. The opening hours are long enough and quiet. If you don't want to leave the hotel, you can stay for a day to handle work and solve the problem of food.

In terms of service, the hotel's level exceeded my expectations. When checking in, different gifts were prepared for the two children, and the little ones loved them. During the stay, every time we entered the room to clean, the hotel would contact us by phone or WeChat to see if it was convenient (this respect for guest privacy is not something that every hotel can do); the most thoughtful thing was that because we took an early flight on the day of departure, the housekeeper Vivian prepared a rich breakfast in advance and packed it for us to take away. Considering the different tastes of adults and children, the last item left in the room was also arranged to be mailed as soon as possible.

It may be too exaggerated to be called "seven stars", but overall, Wuhan Wanda Ruihua is definitely worthy of more than five stars.
